                  <script>
                   $(document).on('change', '.towoptions', function(e) {
     if ($('#notknowtow').is(':checked')) {
         $.ajax({
             beforeSend: function() {
                 $('#process_spinner.ajax-modal').show();
             },
             complete: function() {
                 $('#process_spinner.ajax-modal').hide();
             },
             url: '/towguidedate',
             type: 'GET'
         })
 
           .done(function( msg ) {
             years = JSON.parse(msg);
             var yearHTML = "";
             yearHTML += "<option value=''>Select Year</option>";
                 for(var i = 0; i < years.length; i++) {
                     yearHTML += "<option value='"+years[i]+"''>"+years[i]+"</option>";
                 }
              $("#yeardate").html(yearHTML);
           });
 
        
     }
 });
                  </script>

                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Popular for those who need lightweight units
                  </li>
                  <li>

                  </li>

             <div class="pop-title">
              A-Frame
             </div>
             <div class="carousel-wrapper">
              <div class="carousel">
               <div class="col" data-index="1" data-scroll="1">
                <div class="img">
                 <a href="#">
                  <img alt="1" data-src="https://res.cloudinary.com/camping-world/image/upload/q_auto,f_auto,fl_lossy/imagesrvscom/content/aframe/4.svg"/>
                 </a>
                </div>
                <div class="text">
                 <span class="text-title">
                  A-Frame
                 </span>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   Folds down for easy storage and towing
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Small and light enough to be towed by a minivan or SUV
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Security and insulation of a hard sided trailer
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   No canvas to care for or dry off after a camping trip
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Typically sleeps up to 4 people
                  </li>
                 </ul>
                </div>

                </div>

                 <span class="text-title">
                  A-Frame
                 </span>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   Folds down for easy storage and towing
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Small and light enough to be towed by a minivan or SUV
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Security and insulation of a hard sided trailer
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   No canvas to care for or dry off after a camping trip
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   Typically sleeps up to 4 people
                  </li>
                 </ul>

   <script>
    $(function() {
 		var hoursCount = 3;
 		var business_group = 'Camping World RV Sales';
 		if (business_group =='Gander RV Sales'){
 			if (hoursCount >= 2){
 				$('#dealerHours').css('width','80%');
 			}else{
 				$('#dealerHours').css('width','40%');
 			}
 		}else{
 			if (hoursCount >= 3){
 			$('.storehours').addClass('col-lg-4 col-sm-4 col-xs-12 ');
 			} else if (hoursCount == 2){
 				$('.storehours').addClass('col-lg-6 col-sm-6 col-xs-12 ');
 			} else {
 				$('.storehours').addClass('col-lg-12 col-md-12 col-sm-12 col-xs-12 ');
 			}
 		}
 
 		
 
 	//can-1124
 	var newused = "new";
 	var type = "";
 	var locations = 'CH';
 	var dealerMetro = 'chattanooga';
 	var dealerState = 'tennessee';
 	var dealerCity = 'chattanooga';
 
 	var storeType = 'dealer';
 
 	if(storeType === "dealer"){
 		$.get('/api/make-brand/',{newused:newused,category:type,locations:locations},function(data){
 			var count = 0;
 			var returnHTML = "";
             var useOffset = false;
             var offset = "col-lg-offset-1 col-md-offset-1";
 
 		$.each(data, function(make, brands) {
 				if(count % 5 == 0){
 					useOffset = true;
 				} else {
                     useOffset = false;
                 }
 
 				var dealerString = "";
 
 				var locationName = "Chattanooga";
 				var globalSBSOnCw = ["Tom Johnson Camping","Jamatt RV","AIRSTREAM OF VIRGINIA","McGeorge RV","Ketelsen Campers of Colorado","Nelsons RVs","RV World of Georgia","RV World of Virginia","Jack Sisemore Traveland","America Choice Bushnell","America Choice Ocala","New Prairie RV","River City RVs","Cullum & Maxey RVs","America Choice Winter Garden","B and B RV","Leisure Time RV"];
 
 				if(jQuery.inArray(locationName, globalSBSOnCw)){
 					dealerString = locationName.toLowerCase() + '-' + dealerState + '-' + dealerCity
 				}
 				else if(dealerMetro !== dealerCity){
 					dealerString = dealerMetro + '-' + dealerState + '-' + dealerCity
 				}else{
 					dealerString = dealerMetro + '-' + dealerState;
 				}
 
                 var brandsList = "";
 				$.each(brands, function(key, brand) {
 					brandsList += '<li><a href="/product/' + make.toLowerCase().replace(/\s/g,"-") + '/' + brand.toLowerCase().replace(/\s/g,"-") + '/dealer/' + dealerString + '">' + brand.toLowerCase() + '</a></li>';
 				});
 
                 var offsetCSS = useOffset ? offset : "";
 
                 returnHTML +=
                             '<div class="col-lg-2 col-md-2 col-sm-12 col-xs-12 ' +  offsetCSS  + '"> \
                                 <div class="col-lg-12 col-lg-offset-0 col-md-11 col-md-offset-1 col-sm-7 col-sm-offset-5 col-xs-9 col-xs-offset-2"> \
                                     <h2><a href="/product/' + make.toLowerCase().replace(/\s/g,"-") + '/dealer/' + dealerString + '">' + make.toLowerCase() + '</a></h2> \
                                     <ul>'+brandsList+'</ul>\
                                 </div> \
                             </div>';
                 count++;
 
 			});
 
 			if(count !== 0){
 				$("#popularBrands .popular-brands").html(returnHTML);
 				$("#popularBrands").removeClass("hide");
 
                 var divs = $("div.popular-brands > div");
                 for(var i = 0; i < divs.length; i+=5) {
                 divs.slice(i, i+5).wrapAll("<div class='row items-row'></div>");
                 }
 
 
 
 			}else{
 				$("#popularBrands").remove();
 			}
 		},"json");
 	}
 
 	$(function() {
 		// all-283
 		$(".glCodeLink").on("click touchstart", function(e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			var glCode = 'CH';
 			buildGLCodeLink($(this).attr('href'), glCode);
 		});
 
 
 		function buildGLCodeLink(link, glCode){
 			functions.setCookie('cw_selectedDealer', glCode, 30, true);
 
 			setTimeout(function(){
 					window.location = link + "?forcegl="+glCode;
 			},1000);
 		}
 
 	});
 
     $(".paPopover").on("click touchstart", function(e){

     $(document).on('click', function (e) {
         $('[data-toggle="popover"]').each(function () {
         	//the 'is' for buttons that trigger popups
         	//the 'has' for icons within a button that triggers a popup
             if (!$(this).is(e.target) && $(this).has(e.target).length === 0 && $('.popover').has(e.target).length === 0) {
                 (($(this).popover('hide').data('bs.popover')||{}).inState||{}).click = false  // fix for BS 3.3.6
             }

   <script async="" defer="" src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?onload=onloadCallback&amp;render=explicit">
   </script>
   <script>
    var reCaptchaList = function(){
 		var list = [];
 
 		var push = function(obj){
 			list.push(obj);
 		}
 
 		var getCaptchaIDWhereDivIDEquals = function(divID){
 			for (var i=0; i < list.length; i++) {
 				if (list[i].divID === divID) {
 					return list[i].reCaptchaID;
 				}
 			}
 		}
 
 		var getList = function(){
 			return list;
 		}
 
 		return {
 			push : push,
 			getCaptchaIDWhereDivIDEquals : getCaptchaIDWhereDivIDEquals,
 			getList: getList
 		}
 	}();
 
 	var reCaptchaExecute = function(){
 
 		var execute = function(parentDiv){
 			if($.isValid(parentDiv)){
 				var divID = $(parentDiv).find('.invisibleRecaptcha').attr('id');
 				var id = reCaptchaList.getCaptchaIDWhereDivIDEquals(divID);
 
 				grecaptcha.execute(id);
 			}
 		}
 
 		return {
 			execute : execute,
 		}
 
 	}();
 
 	var recaptchaCount = 0;
 
 	var onloadCallback = function() {
 	    var recaptchaSiteKey = '6LfMey8UAAAAAJz09vPXwlIS5ixb7_Xnna7fV4kc';
 		//each div needs to have the data-submit for the callback function.
 
 		$('.invisibleRecaptcha').each(function(index){
 			var curDivID = $(this).attr("id") + '_' + recaptchaCount.toString();
 			$(this).attr("id", curDivID);
 			
 			$(this).attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
 			$(this).attr('aria-label', 'recaptcha');
 			$(this).attr('aria-readonly', 'true');
 
 			$(this).before(function () {
 				return $('<label />', {
 					for: 'g-recaptcha-response',
 					text: 'recaptcha label do not read',
 					hide: true
 				}).append(this.previousSibling)
 			});
 
 
 			callBack = $(this).data('submit');
 			reCaptchaID = grecaptcha.render($(this).attr("id"),{
 				"sitekey": recaptchaSiteKey,
 				"badge": "inline",
 				"type": "image",
 				"size": "invisible",
 				"callback": callBack
 			});
 
 			reCaptchaList.push({
 				divID : $(this).attr("id"),
 				reCaptchaID : reCaptchaID
 			});
 			recaptchaCount++;
 		});
 	};
 
 	var renderModalRecaptcha = function(c) {
 		var recaptchaSiteKey = '6LfMey8UAAAAAJz09vPXwlIS5ixb7_Xnna7fV4kc';
 		//each div needs to have the data-submit for the callback function.
 
 		$(c).find('.invisibleRecaptchaModal').each(function(index){
 			var curDivID = $(this).attr("id") + '_' + recaptchaCount.toString();
 			$(this).attr("id", curDivID);
 			
 			$(this).attr('aria-hidden', 'true');
 			$(this).attr('aria-label', 'recaptcha');
 			$(this).attr('aria-readonly', 'true');
 
 			$(this).before(function () {
 				return $('<label />', {
 					for: 'g-recaptcha-response',
 					text: 'recaptcha label do not read',
 					hide: true
 				}).append(this.previousSibling)
 			});
 
 			callBack = $(this).data('submit');
 			reCaptchaID = grecaptcha.render($(this).attr("id"),{
 				"sitekey": recaptchaSiteKey,
 				"badge": "inline",
 				"type": "image",
 				"size": "invisible",
 				"callback": callBack
 			});
 
 			reCaptchaList.push({
 				divID : $(this).attr("id"),
 				reCaptchaID : reCaptchaID
 			});
 			$(this).removeClass("invisibleRecaptchaModal");
 			$(this).addClass("invisibleRecaptcha");
 			recaptchaCount++;
 		});
 	};
   </script>

    <script>
     //standalones should not show on the modal
 //$('.standalone').remove();
 //When page loads, check for cookie
 	if(Cookies.get('cw_searchByZip')=='true'){
 		$('#'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).prependTo('.dealerlist');
 		$('#zipsearch_store').val(Cookies.get('cw_searchZipcode'));
 		getZipClosest();
 		$('.bs-choosedealer-modal-lg #glyph_remove').show();
 		$('.bs-choosedealer-modal-lg #glyph_search').hide();
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).removeClass('choose-dealer');
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).addClass('my-dealer');
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).html("My Dealer");
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).closest('i').removeClass('store-star');
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).closest('i').addClass('store-star-selected');
 		//$('.store-star.'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).click();
 	}
 	else if(Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')){
 		$('#'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).prependTo('.dealerlist');
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).removeClass('choose-dealer');
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).addClass('my-dealer');
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).html("My Dealer");
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).closest('i').removeClass('store-star');
 		$('#choose'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).closest('i').addClass('store-star-selected');
 		//$('.store-star.'+Cookies.get('cw_selectedDealer')).click();
 		$('#process_spinner.ajax-modal').hide();
 	}
 	else{
 		$('#process_spinner.ajax-modal').hide();
 	}
    </script>
